On selection, navigates to the region and unfolds it if collapsed\n    4. Centers the view on the selected region\n\n- Registered the action with `registerEditorAction(GoToNamedRegionAction)`\n\n## Design Decisions\n\n### 1. Region Detection Pattern\nUsed regex patterns to detect `#region` markers:\n- Supports multiple comment styles\n- Extracts region name from the marker\n- Handles trailing comment delimiters (`*/`)\n\n### 2. Users can now mark code sections with special comments and navigate between them using a quick-pick menu.\n\n## Quick Start\n\n### Using Named Regions\n\n1. **Mark regions in your code:**\n   ```typescript\n   // #region Setup\n   const config = loadConfig();\n   const database = initDatabase();\n   // #endregion\n\n   // #region Main Logic\n   function main() {\n     // Implementation\n   }\n   // #endregion\n   ```\n\n2. **Open the region menu:**\n   - Press `Ctrl+Shift+R` (Windows/Linux) or `Cmd+Shift+R` (Mac)\n   - Or use the Command Palette: \"Go to Named Region\"\n\n3. **Select a region** from the quick-pick menu to navigate to it\n\n## Features\n\n✅ **Region Detection**\n- Automatically detects `#region <name>` and `#endregion` markers\n- Supports multiple comment styles:\n  - Line comments: `// #region MySection`\n  - Block comments: `/* #region MyBlock */`\n  - Python/Shell: `# #region MySection`\n\n✅ **Quick Navigation**\n- Shows all named regions in a quick-pick menu\n- Displays region name and line number range\n- Navigates to selected region\n- Automatically unfolds collapsed regions\n\n✅ **Smart Features**\n- Handles nested regions correctly\n- Respects VS Code's folding region limits\n- Properly extracts region names with spaces and special characters\n- Gracefully handles edge cases (unmatched markers, no regions)\n\n## Implementation Details\n\n### Files Created\n\n1. **`src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/namedRangeProvider.ts`**\n   - Core provider for named region detection\n   - Implements `RangeProvider` interface\n   - Exports `NamedRegion` interface and `computeNamedRanges()` function\n\n2. **`src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/test/browser/namedRangeProvider.test.ts`**\n   - Comprehensive test suite with 8 test cases\n   - Tests region detection, name extraction, and edge cases\n\n### Files Modified\n\n1. **`src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/folding.ts`**\n   - Added `GoToNamedRegionAction` class\n   - Registered command: `editor.action.goToNamedRegion`\n   - Added keybinding: `Ctrl+Shift+R`\n\n## Command Reference\n\n- **Command ID:** `editor.action.goToNamedRegion`\n- **Title:** Go to Named Region\n- **Keybinding:**\n  - Windows/Linux: `Ctrl+Shift+R`\n  - Mac: `Cmd+Shift+R`\n- **When:** Editor has text focus\n\n## Architecture\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│      GoToNamedRegionAction              │\n│   (Registered EditorAction)             │\n└──────────────┬──────────────────────────┘\n               │\n               ├─→ NamedRangeProvider\n               │   - Detects #region markers\n               │   - Extracts region names\n               │   - Returns FoldingRegions\n               │\n               ├─→ QuickInputService\n               │   - Shows quick-pick menu\n               │   - Lists all regions\n               │\n               └─→ FoldingModel\n                   - Unfolds selected region\n                   - Manages collapse state\n```\n\n## Testing\n\nThe implementation includes a comprehensive test suite covering:\n\n1. Single and multiple named regions\n2. Nested regions\n3. Region names with spaces\n4. Different comment styles\n5. Edge cases:\n   - No regions in document\n   - Unmatched endregion markers\n   - Region limit handling\n\nRun tests with:\n```bash\nnpm run test-browser-no-install\n```\n\n## Design Decisions\n\n### Why `#region` Markers?\nVS Code already uses `#region`/`#endregion` markers for native folding, so using the same syntax is intuitive and familiar to users.\n\n### Why a Quick-Pick Menu?\nQuick-pick provides:\n- Visual list of all regions\n- Search capability (by region name)\n- Line number information\n- Accessible keybinding\n\n### Why Dynamic Import?\nThe `computeNamedRanges` function is imported dynamically in the action to:\n- Reduce initial bundle size\n- Load only when command is used\n- Follow VS Code's async patterns\n\n## Compatibility\n\n- **Supported Languages:** All languages that support comment syntax\n- **VS Code Version:** 1.96.0 and above\n- **Folding Strategy:** Works with any folding strategy (indentation, syntax)\n\n## Performance\n\n- Region detection is O(n) where n = number of lines\n- Respects configured folding region limits\n- No impact on editor performance when regions are not used\n\n## Future Enhancements\n\nPotential improvements for future
